\[
f(t,A)= -0.7317701895\,A\,e^{-0.08162134037\,t}\;+\;0.840340505\,\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So GT is exactly ŌĆ£(A times a decaying exponential in \(t\)) + (a pure cosine of \(\log(A+1)\))ŌĆØ, with **no other \(t\)-dependence** and **no other \(A\)-dependence**.

Key structural requirements any candidate must be able to reproduce (possibly after setting some candidate constants to 0, and possibly under a domain condition like \(A\ge 0\)):

1) The \(t\)-dependent part must be exactly \(A\cdot C\cdot e^{k t}\) with \(k=-0.08162134...\) and \(C=-0.731770...\).  
2) The oscillatory part must be exactly \(0.84034...\cos(\log(A+1))\). Candidates that only have \(\sin(\alpha\log(\beta|A|+1)+\phi)\) can match cosine via phase shift, and can match \(\log(A+1)\) by choosing \(\alpha=1,\beta=1\) and using the domain condition \(A\ge 0\) so \(|A|=A\).  
3) Any extra terms (constants, logs, rational terms, extra exponentials, \(t\) polynomials, etc.) must be removable by setting their coefficients to 0.

Now check candidates.

### Candidates 1ŌĆō7
All of 1ŌĆō7 have no trig term of the form \(\sin(\log(\cdot))\) or \(\cos(\log(\cdot))\); they instead have rational/log/pure exponentials in \(A\). Even if we zero out many terms, none can produce \(\cos(\log(A+1))\).  
ŌćÆ 1ŌĆō7 do **not** match.

### Candidate 8
\[
A c_0 e^{c_1 t} + c_2\sin(c_3\log(c_4|A|+1)+c_5)+ \frac{c_6 t}{A c_7+c_8}+\frac{c_9}{A c_7+c_8}
\]
Set \(c_6=0,c_9=0\) to remove rational terms. Then we have:
\[
A c_0 e^{c_1 t} + c_2\sin(c_3\log(c_4|A|+1)+c_5).
\]
Match the exponential term by \(c_1=-0.08162134037\), \(c_0=-0.7317701895\).

Match cosine term using sine phase shift: \(\cos(x)=\sin(x+\pi/2)\).  
Choose domain condition \(A\ge 0\) so \(|A|=A\). Then set \(c_3=1\), \(c_4=1\), \(c_5=\pi/2\), \(c_2=0.84034050498\). This gives:
\[
0.84034\sin(\log(A+1)+\pi/2)=0.84034\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
Exactly GT on \(A\ge 0\) (and also requires \(A>-1\) for the log; GT itself needs \(A>-1\) anyway).  
ŌćÆ **Candidate 8 matches** (conditional equivalence on \(A\ge 0\)).

### Candidate 9
Has extra term \(A c_2\max(0,c_3+t)\) which cannot be made identically 0 for all \(t\) by a domain restriction unless \(c_2=0\). If \(c_2=0\), remaining is \(A c_0 e^{c_1 t}+c_4+c_5\sin(\cdots)\). The constant \(c_4\) must be 0; then it can match similarly to candidate 8. Also has \(\sin(\log(c_7|A|+1)+c_8)\) which can match cosine via phase.  
So with \(c_2=0,c_4=0\) and \(A\ge 0\), it can match.  
ŌćÆ Candidate 9 also matches (but we already have a match).

### Candidate 10
Uses \(c_0 e^{c_1 t}|A|\) (not \(A\)). Under domain \(A\le 0\), \(|A|=-A\) so it becomes \(-c_0 e^{c_1 t}A\), which can match the sign. But it also has \(+c_7 t\) which must be zeroed by \(c_7=0\), and constant \(c_2\) must be 0. Then trig sine(log(|A|)) can match cosine(log(A+1)) only if \(|A|\) can be replaced by \(A\), which would require \(A\ge 0\), conflicting with the \(A\le 0\) used to convert \(|A|\) to \(-A\). If instead take \(A\ge 0\), then \(|A|=A\) but the exponential term is \(+c_0 A e^{c_1 t}\) and we can set \(c_0=-0.73177\) anyway, so no conflict. Then trig matches as before.  
ŌćÆ Candidate 10 can match on \(A\ge 0\) with \(c_7=0,c_2=0\) and phase shift.

### Candidate 11

### Candidate 12

ŌćÆ Matches.

### Candidate 13

ŌćÆ Matches.

### Candidate 14ŌĆō104 (summary)
Many later candidates include the needed building blocks \(A c_0 e^{c_1 t}\) and \(\sin(\log(c|A|+1)+\phi)\) plus extra terms that can be zeroed by setting coefficients to 0. Those can match under \(A\ge 0\) with the same parameter choices (and phase shift).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK7)

GT: -c0*A*exp(-c1*_s*t) + c2*_w*cos(log(A + c3))
Candidate formulas: 104

GT (fixed):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.7317701895\,A\,e^{-0.08162134037\,t} \;+\; 0.840340505\,\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able to represent **(i)** an \(A\cdot e^{k t}\) term with \(k=-0.0816213\) and coefficient \(-0.73177\), and **(ii)** a pure cosine of \(\log(A+1)\) with amplitude \(0.84034\), with **no extra dependence** on \(t\) or \(A\) beyond those two terms (extra terms must be zeroable by parameter choices). Also note \(\cos(x)=\sin(x+\pi/2)\), and \(\log(c\cdot|A|+1)\) can match \(\log(A+1)\) under domain \(A\ge 0\) with \(c=1\).

Now check candidates.

1ŌĆō7: These have \(A c_0 e^{c_1 t}\) (good for the first GT term by setting \(c_0=-0.73177, c_1=-0.0816213\)), but their remaining parts are rational/log terms in \(A\), not a sinusoid/cosine of \(\log(A+1)\). No way to turn rational/log into cosine. ŌćÆ no.

8: \(A c_0 e^{c_1 t} + c_2\sin(c_3\log(c_4|A|+1)+c_5)+\frac{c_6 t}{A c_7+c_8}+\frac{c_9}{A c_7+c_8}\).
- Set \(c_0=-0.7317701895,\; c_1=-0.08162134037\).
- Kill extra rational terms: set \(c_6=0,\; c_9=0\) (then those fractions vanish regardless of \(c_7,c_8\), assuming denominator nonzero on domain).
- Match cosine term via sine phase shift and argument scaling:
  - Need \(\sin(\,\log(A+1)+\pi/2\,)=\cos(\log(A+1))\).
  - Choose domain condition \(A\ge 0\) so \(|A|=A\).
